#### What this PR does / why we need it:
In order to facilitate the review and to be able to quickly merge. I split the implementation into multiple prs.
This pr is `add UnscheduleQ in the internal ClusterQueue struct.`

## Discussion

### Comment by [@denkensk](https://github.com/denkensk) — 2022-03-22T10:47:18Z

> I prefer not to merge this on its own, but we can iterate over it, and then once "lgmted" we add another commit to the same PR with the reset of the implementation, why do you think?

sgtm. I add the reset of the implementation in this commit. I've tested it in a real cluster to make sure it works.
Pls take a look.  @ahg-g @alculquicondor 

And integration test will be added in the follow-up commit in this pr.

### Comment by [@denkensk](https://github.com/denkensk) — 2022-03-25T09:02:09Z

> More immediate, we should document all events that could make a workload admissible, this is helpful to cross check if we actually covered all cases (and typically a test for each case).

Thanks @ahg-g  I copy from https://docs.google.com/document/d/1VQ0qxWA-jwgvLq_WYG46OkXWW00O6q7b1BsR_Uv-acs/edit?usp=sharing I documented it before.

It is similar to the implementation of the default-scheduler, we need to trigger the re-queue operation based on the relevant events.

1. workloads deleted event --> move all the workloads in the same cohort back to heap.
2. cluster queue added event --> move all the workloads in the same cohort back to heap.
3. cluster queue updated event --> move all the workloads in the same cohort back to heap.

The first version a rough and simple operation. Next step, we need to select the workloads to move based on the exact event in the next step, like RequestableResources / NamespaceSelector / Cohort changed ....

### Comment by [@denkensk](https://github.com/denkensk) — 2022-03-25T09:05:42Z

> It would be nice if we can come up with an "interface" for QueueingStrategy that each queueing strategy implements and gets invoked agnostically by queue manager. This will allow us to establish a clear framework for when the queueing strategy could impact the logic rather than hardcoding things per strategy all over the place.

I created a new pr to come up with an `interface` of ClusterQueue https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/pull/146
After it's merged. I will inherit the base implementation to refactor the `besteffortFIFO`.

### Comment by [@ahg-g](https://github.com/ahg-g) — 2022-03-25T19:09:18Z

> It is similar to the implementation of the default-scheduler, we need to trigger the re-queue operation based on the relevant events.
> 
> 1. workloads deleted event --> move all the workloads in the same cohort back to heap.
> 2. cluster queue added event --> move all the workloads in the same cohort back to heap.
> 3. cluster queue updated event --> move all the workloads in the same cohort back to heap.

can we please document those in the code.

### Review by [@ahg-g](https://github.com/ahg-g) (commented) — 2022-03-21T15:45:48Z

I prefer not to merge this on its own, but we can iterate over it, and then once "lgmted" we add another commit to the same PR with the reset of the implementation, why do you think?

- **api/v1alpha1/clusterqueue_types.go:162** by [@ahg-g](https://github.com/ahg-g) — 2022-03-21T15:21:31Z
```diff
@@ -156,6 +157,10 @@ type QueueingStrategy string
 const (
 	// StrictFIFO means that workloads are sorted strictly by creation time.
 	StrictFIFO QueueingStrategy = "StrictFIFO"
+
+	// BestEffortFIFO means that workloads are sorted based on creation time
+	// with event-based re-queueing.
```

  "with event-based re-queueing." is an implementation detail, can we describe the semantics in a different way? like: "Workloads will be admitted based on their creation time, however older workloads that can't be admitted will not block newer ones that can"

- **api/v1alpha1/clusterqueue_types.go:158** by [@ahg-g](https://github.com/ahg-g) — 2022-03-21T15:22:32Z
```diff
@@ -156,6 +157,10 @@ type QueueingStrategy string
 const (
 	// StrictFIFO means that workloads are sorted strictly by creation time.
```

  clarify: To preserve strict FIFO semantics, workloads that can't be admitted will block admitting newer workloads that can.

- **pkg/queue/queue.go:249** by [@ahg-g](https://github.com/ahg-g) — 2022-03-21T15:44:33Z
```diff
@@ -213,3 +222,49 @@ func (h *heapImpl) Pop() interface{} {
 	delete(h.items, key)
 	return obj
 }
+
+// UnschedulableWorkloadsMap implementation inspired by
+// https://github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes/blob/master/pkg/scheduler/internal/queue/queue.go
+
+// UnschedulableWorkloadsMap holds workloads that cannot be scheduled.
+// This data structure is used to implement unschedulableQ.
+type UnschedulableWorkloadsMap struct {
+	// workloadInfoMap is a map key by a workload's full-name and the value
+	// is a/pointer to the workload.Info.
+	workloadInfoMap map[string]*workload.Info
+}
+
+// Add adds a workload to the unschedulable workloadInfoMap.
+func (u *UnschedulableWorkloadsMap) addOrUpdate(wInfo *workload.Info) {
+	key := workload.Key(wInfo.Obj)
+	u.workloadInfoMap[key] = wInfo
+}
+
+// Delete deletes a workload from the unschedulable workloadInfoMap.
+func (u *UnschedulableWorkloadsMap) delete(w *kueue.QueuedWorkload) {
+	key := workload.Key(w)
+	delete(u.workloadInfoMap, key)
+}
+
+// TODO unused now
```

  non of the others are used as well :)
  
  I suggest we either uncomment and unit test it or remove this code.

### Review by [@ahg-g](https://github.com/ahg-g) (commented) — 2022-03-22T11:42:32Z

Thanks Alex, this is great as a first initial implementation. I have a couple of macro comments:

1) It would be nice if we can come up with an "interface" for QueueingStrategy that each queueing strategy implements and gets invoked agnostically by queue manager. This will allow us to establish a clear framework for when the queueing strategy could impact the logic rather than hardcoding things per strategy all over the place.

2) More immediate, we should document all events that could make a workload admissible, this is helpful to cross check if we actually covered all cases (and typically a test for each case).

- **api/v1alpha1/clusterqueue_types.go:140** by [@ahg-g](https://github.com/ahg-g) — 2022-03-22T11:09:48Z
```diff
@@ -137,10 +137,11 @@ type ClusterQueueSpec struct {
 	// across the queues in this ClusterQueue. This field is immutable.
 	// Current Supported Strategies:
 	//
-	// - StrictFIFO: workloads are sorted strictly by creation time.
+	// - StrictFIFO: workloads are sorted strictly by creation time. And older workloads that can't be admitted will block admitting newer workloads that can.
```

  ```suggestion
  	// - StrictFIFO: workloads are ordered strictly by creation time. Older workloads that can't be admitted 
  	//                       will block admitting newer workloads even if they fit available quota.
  ```

- **api/v1alpha1/clusterqueue_types.go:141** by [@ahg-g](https://github.com/ahg-g) — 2022-03-22T11:10:39Z
```diff
@@ -137,10 +137,11 @@ type ClusterQueueSpec struct {
 	// across the queues in this ClusterQueue. This field is immutable.
 	// Current Supported Strategies:
 	//
-	// - StrictFIFO: workloads are sorted strictly by creation time.
+	// - StrictFIFO: workloads are sorted strictly by creation time. And older workloads that can't be admitted will block admitting newer workloads that can.
+	// - BestEffortFIFO：workloads are sorted strictly by creation time, however older workloads that can't be admitted will not block admitting newer workloads that can.
```

  ```suggestion
  	// - BestEffortFIFO：workloads are ordered by creation time, however older workloads that can't be 
  	//                                 admitted will not block admitting newer workloads that fit existing quota.
  ```

- **api/v1alpha1/clusterqueue_types.go:170** by [@ahg-g](https://github.com/ahg-g) — 2022-03-22T11:12:16Z
```diff
@@ -155,7 +156,14 @@ type QueueingStrategy string
 
 const (
 	// StrictFIFO means that workloads are sorted strictly by creation time.
+	// And older workloads that can't be admitted will block admitting newer
+	// workloads that can.
 	StrictFIFO QueueingStrategy = "StrictFIFO"
+
+	// BestEffortFIFO means that workloads are sorted strictly by creation time,
+	// however older workloads that can't be admitted will not block
+	// admitting newer workloads that can.
+	BestEffortFIFO QueueingStrategy = "BestEffortFIFO"
```

  please update the docs similar to the suggestions made above.

- **pkg/queue/queue.go:185** by [@ahg-g](https://github.com/ahg-g) — 2022-03-22T11:32:49Z
```diff
@@ -149,6 +169,56 @@ func (cq *ClusterQueue) Pop() *workload.Info {
 	return &w
 }
 
+func (cq *ClusterQueue) RequeueWorkload(wInfo *workload.Info) (bool, error) {
+	switch cq.QueueingStrategy {
+	case kueue.StrictFIFO:
+		return cq.PushIfNotPresent(wInfo), nil
+	case kueue.BestEffortFIFO:
+		if err := cq.AddUnschedulableIfNotPresent(wInfo); err != nil {
+			return false, err
+		}
+	}
+	return true, nil
+}
+
+// AddUnschedulableIfNotPresent inserts a workload that cannot be scheduled into
+// the unschedulableWorkloads in ClusterQueue, unless it is already in the queue.
```

  ```suggestion
  // AddInadmissibleIfNotPresent inserts a workload that cannot be admitted into
  // the inadmissibleWorkloads in ClusterQueue, unless it is already in the queue.
  ```

- **pkg/queue/queue.go:201** by [@ahg-g](https://github.com/ahg-g) — 2022-03-22T11:34:06Z
```diff
@@ -149,6 +169,56 @@ func (cq *ClusterQueue) Pop() *workload.Info {
 	return &w
 }
 
+func (cq *ClusterQueue) RequeueWorkload(wInfo *workload.Info) (bool, error) {
+	switch cq.QueueingStrategy {
+	case kueue.StrictFIFO:
+		return cq.PushIfNotPresent(wInfo), nil
+	case kueue.BestEffortFIFO:
+		if err := cq.AddUnschedulableIfNotPresent(wInfo); err != nil {
+			return false, err
+		}
+	}
+	return true, nil
+}
+
+// AddUnschedulableIfNotPresent inserts a workload that cannot be scheduled into
+// the unschedulableWorkloads in ClusterQueue, unless it is already in the queue.
+func (cq *ClusterQueue) AddUnschedulableIfNotPresent(wInfo *workload.Info) error {
+	w := wInfo.Obj
+	if cq.unschedulableWorkloads.get(w) != nil {
+		return fmt.Errorf("workload %v is already present in unschedulableWorkloads", workload.Key(w))
+	}
+
+	if _, exist := cq.heap.Get(wInfo); exist {
+		return fmt.Errorf("workload %v is already present in the clusterqueue heap", workload.Key(w))
+	}
+
+	cq.unschedulableWorkloads.addOrUpdate(wInfo)
+	return nil
+}
+
+// MoveAllToClusterQueue moves all workloads from unschedulableWorkloads to heap.
+func (cq *ClusterQueue) MoveAllToClusterQueue() {
```

  ```suggestion
  func (cq *ClusterQueue) QueueAllInadmissibleWorkloads() {
  ```

```diff
+
```
```diff
+package queue
```

```diff
+import (
+	"container/heap"
+	"fmt"
+
+	kueue "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/api/v1alpha1"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/workload"
+)
+
+// ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO is the implementation for the ClusterQueue for
+// BestEffortFIFO.
+type ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO struct {
+	*ClusterQueueImpl
+
+	// inadmissibleWorkloads are workloads that have been tried at least once and couldn't be admitted.
+	inadmissibleWorkloads *InadmissibleWorkloads
+}
+
+var _ ClusterQueue = &ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO{}
+
+const BestEffortFIFO = kueue.BestEffortFIFO
+
+func newClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO(cq *kueue.ClusterQueue) (ClusterQueue, error) {
+	cqImpl := ClusterQueueImpl{
+		heap: heapImpl{
+			less:  strictFIFO,
+			items: make(map[string]*heapItem),
+		},
+	}
+
+	cqBE := &ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO{
+		ClusterQueueImpl:      &cqImpl,
+		inadmissibleWorkloads: newInadmissibleWorkloads(),
+	}
+
+	cqBE.Update(cq)
+	return cqBE, nil
+}
+
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) PushOrUpdate(w *kueue.QueuedWorkload) {
+	if oldInfo := cq.inadmissibleWorkloads.get(w); oldInfo != nil {
+		cq.inadmissibleWorkloads.delete(w)
+	}
+
+	item := cq.heap.items[workload.Key(w)]
+	info := *workload.NewInfo(w)
+	if item == nil {
+		heap.Push(&cq.heap, info)
+		return
+	}
+	item.obj = info
+	heap.Fix(&cq.heap, item.index)
```

- **pkg/queue/clsuter_queue_best_effort_fifo.go:138** by [@ahg-g](https://github.com/ahg-g) — 2022-03-26T13:38:22Z
```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,163 @@
+/*
+Copyright 2022 The Kubernetes Authors.
+
+Licensed under the Apache License, Version 2.0 (the "License");
+you may not use this file except in compliance with the License.
+You may obtain a copy of the License at
+
+    http://www.apache.org/licenses/LICENSE-2.0
+
+Unless required by applicable law or agreed to in writing, software
+distributed under the License is distributed on an "AS IS" BASIS,
+WITHOUT WARRANTIES OR CONDITIONS OF ANY KIND, either express or implied.
+See the License for the specific language governing permissions and
+limitations under the License.
+*/
+
+package queue
+
+import (
+	"container/heap"
+	"fmt"
+
+	kueue "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/api/v1alpha1"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/workload"
+)
+
+// ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO is the implementation for the ClusterQueue for
+// BestEffortFIFO.
+type ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO struct {
+	*ClusterQueueImpl
+
+	// inadmissibleWorkloads are workloads that have been tried at least once and couldn't be admitted.
+	inadmissibleWorkloads *InadmissibleWorkloads
+}
+
+var _ ClusterQueue = &ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO{}
+
+const BestEffortFIFO = kueue.BestEffortFIFO
+
+func newClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO(cq *kueue.ClusterQueue) (ClusterQueue, error) {
+	cqImpl := ClusterQueueImpl{
+		heap: heapImpl{
+			less:  strictFIFO,
+			items: make(map[string]*heapItem),
+		},
+	}
+
+	cqBE := &ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO{
+		ClusterQueueImpl:      &cqImpl,
+		inadmissibleWorkloads: newInadmissibleWorkloads(),
+	}
+
+	cqBE.Update(cq)
+	return cqBE, nil
+}
+
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) PushOrUpdate(w *kueue.QueuedWorkload) {
+	if oldInfo := cq.inadmissibleWorkloads.get(w); oldInfo != nil {
+		cq.inadmissibleWorkloads.delete(w)
+	}
+
+	item := cq.heap.items[workload.Key(w)]
+	info := *workload.NewInfo(w)
+	if item == nil {
+		heap.Push(&cq.heap, info)
+		return
+	}
+	item.obj = info
+	heap.Fix(&cq.heap, item.index)
+}
+
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) Delete(w *kueue.QueuedWorkload) {
+	item := cq.heap.items[workload.Key(w)]
+	if item != nil {
+		heap.Remove(&cq.heap, item.index)
+	}
+
+	cq.inadmissibleWorkloads.delete(w)
+}
+
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) RequeueWorkload(wInfo *workload.Info) (bool, error) {
+	if err := cq.AddInadmissibleIfNotPresent(wInfo); err != nil {
+		return false, err
+	}
+	return true, nil
+}
+
+// AddInadmissibleIfNotPresent inserts a workload that cannot be admitted into
+// the inadmissibleWorkloads in ClusterQueue, unless it is already in the queue.
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) AddInadmissibleIfNotPresent(wInfo *workload.Info) error {
+	w := wInfo.Obj
+	if cq.inadmissibleWorkloads.get(w) != nil {
+		return fmt.Errorf("workload %v is already present in inadmissibleWorkloads", workload.Key(w))
+	}
+
+	if _, exist := cq.heap.Get(wInfo); exist {
+		return fmt.Errorf("workload %v is already present in the clusterqueue heap", workload.Key(w))
+	}
+
+	cq.inadmissibleWorkloads.addOrUpdate(wInfo)
+	return nil
+}
+
+// QueueAllInadmissibleWorkloads moves all workloads from inadmissibleWorkloads to heap.
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) QueueAllInadmissibleWorkloads() bool {
+	inadmissibleWorkloads := make([]*workload.Info, 0, len(cq.inadmissibleWorkloads.workloads))
+	for _, pInfo := range cq.inadmissibleWorkloads.workloads {
+		inadmissibleWorkloads = append(inadmissibleWorkloads, pInfo)
+	}
+	queued := false
+	for _, wInfo := range inadmissibleWorkloads {
+		w := wInfo.Obj
+		heap.Push(&cq.heap, *wInfo)
+		cq.inadmissibleWorkloads.delete(w)
+		queued = true
+	}
+	return queued
+}
+
+// InadmissibleWorkloads implementation inspired by
+// https://github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes/blob/master/pkg/scheduler/internal/queue/queue.go
+
+// InadmissibleWorkloads holds workloads that cannot be scheduled.
+// This data structure is used to implement inadmissibleWorkloads.
+type InadmissibleWorkloads struct {
+	// workloads is a map key by a workload's full-name and the value
+	// is a/pointer to the workload.Info.
+	workloads map[string]*workload.Info
+}
+
+// Add adds a workload to the workloads.
+func (i *InadmissibleWorkloads) addOrUpdate(wInfo *workload.Info) {
+	key := workload.Key(wInfo.Obj)
+	i.workloads[key] = wInfo
+}
+
+// Delete deletes a workload from the workloads.
+func (i *InadmissibleWorkloads) delete(w *kueue.QueuedWorkload) {
```

  Input parameter should be the string key only, not the whole type. Same thing with the get function below

```diff
+		heap: heapImpl{

+	}
+
+	cqBE := &ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO{
+		ClusterQueueImpl:      &cqImpl,
+		inadmissibleWorkloads: newInadmissibleWorkloads(),
+	}
+
+	cqBE.Update(cq)
+	return cqBE, nil
+}
+
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) PushOrUpdate(w *kueue.QueuedWorkload) {
+	if oldInfo := cq.inadmissibleWorkloads.get(w); oldInfo != nil {
+		cq.inadmissibleWorkloads.delete(w)
+	}
+
+	item := cq.heap.items[workload.Key(w)]
+	info := *workload.NewInfo(w)
+	if item == nil {
+		heap.Push(&cq.heap, info)
+		return
+	}
+	item.obj = info
+	heap.Fix(&cq.heap, item.index)
+}
+
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) Delete(w *kueue.QueuedWorkload) {
+	item := cq.heap.items[workload.Key(w)]
+	if item != nil {
+		heap.Remove(&cq.heap, item.index)
+	}
+
+	cq.inadmissibleWorkloads.delete(w)
+}
+
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) RequeueWorkload(wInfo *workload.Info) (bool, error) {
+	if err := cq.AddInadmissibleIfNotPresent(wInfo); err != nil {
+		return false, err
+	}
+	return true, nil
+}
+
+// AddInadmissibleIfNotPresent inserts a workload that cannot be admitted into
+// the inadmissibleWorkloads in ClusterQueue, unless it is already in the queue.
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) AddInadmissibleIfNotPresent(wInfo *workload.Info) error {
+	w := wInfo.Obj
+	if cq.inadmissibleWorkloads.get(w) != nil {
+		return fmt.Errorf("workload %v is already present in inadmissibleWorkloads", workload.Key(w))
+	}
+
+	if _, exist := cq.heap.Get(wInfo); exist {
+		return fmt.Errorf("workload %v is already present in the clusterqueue heap", workload.Key(w))
+	}
+
+	cq.inadmissibleWorkloads.addOrUpdate(wInfo)
+	return nil
+}
+
+// QueueAllInadmissibleWorkloads moves all workloads from inadmissibleWorkloads to heap.
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) QueueAllInadmissibleWorkloads() bool {
+	inadmissibleWorkloads := make([]*workload.Info, 0, len(cq.inadmissibleWorkloads.workloads))
+	for _, pInfo := range cq.inadmissibleWorkloads.workloads {
+		inadmissibleWorkloads = append(inadmissibleWorkloads, pInfo)
+	}
+	queued := false
+	for _, wInfo := range inadmissibleWorkloads {
+		w := wInfo.Obj
+		heap.Push(&cq.heap, *wInfo)
+		cq.inadmissibleWorkloads.delete(w)
+		queued = true
+	}
+	return queued
+}
+
+// InadmissibleWorkloads implementation inspired by
+// https://github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes/blob/master/pkg/scheduler/internal/queue/queue.go
+
+// InadmissibleWorkloads holds workloads that cannot be scheduled.
+// This data structure is used to implement inadmissibleWorkloads.
+type InadmissibleWorkloads struct {
+	// workloads is a map key by a workload's full-name and the value
+	// is a/pointer to the workload.Info.
+	workloads map[string]*workload.Info
+}
+
+// Add adds a workload to the workloads.
+func (i *InadmissibleWorkloads) addOrUpdate(wInfo *workload.Info) {
+	key := workload.Key(wInfo.Obj)
+	i.workloads[key] = wInfo
+}
+
+// Delete deletes a workload from the workloads.
+func (i *InadmissibleWorkloads) delete(w *kueue.QueuedWorkload) {
+	key := workload.Key(w)
+	delete(i.workloads, key)
+}
+
+// Get returns the workload.Info if a workload with the same key as the key of the given "workload"
+// is found in the workloads. It returns nil otherwise.
+func (i *InadmissibleWorkloads) get(w *kueue.QueuedWorkload) *workload.Info {
+	key := workload.Key(w)
+	if wInfo, exists := i.workloads[key]; exists {
+		return wInfo
+	}
+	return nil
+}
+
+// Clear removes all the entries from the workloads.
+func (i *InadmissibleWorkloads) clear() {
```

  this seems to be used in the unit test only,  so I would remove the function (just so we offer a smaller api surface) and just do `i.workloads = make(map[string]*workload.Info)` in the unit test itself.

```diff
+type InadmissibleWorkloads struct {
+	// workloads is a map key by a workload's full-name and the value
+	// is a/pointer to the workload.Info.
+	workloads map[string]*workload.Info
+}
+
+// Add adds a workload to the workloads.
+func (i *InadmissibleWorkloads) addOrUpdate(wInfo *workload.Info) {
+	key := workload.Key(wInfo.Obj)
+	i.workloads[key] = wInfo
+}
+
+// Delete deletes a workload from the workloads.
+func (i *InadmissibleWorkloads) delete(w *kueue.QueuedWorkload) {
+	key := workload.Key(w)
+	delete(i.workloads, key)
+}
+
+// Get returns the workload.Info if a workload with the same key as the key of the given "workload"
+// is found in the workloads. It returns nil otherwise.
+func (i *InadmissibleWorkloads) get(w *kueue.QueuedWorkload) *workload.Info {
+	key := workload.Key(w)
+	if wInfo, exists := i.workloads[key]; exists {
+		return wInfo
+	}
+	return nil
+}
+
+// Clear removes all the entries from the workloads.
+func (i *InadmissibleWorkloads) clear() {
+	i.workloads = make(map[string]*workload.Info)
+}
+
+// newInadmissibleWorkloads initializes a new object of InadmissibleWorkloads.
```

  ditto, comment is not explaining anything new and the function is not exported, so I would remove it.

- **pkg/queue/clsuter_queue_best_effort_fifo.go:125** by [@ahg-g](https://github.com/ahg-g) — 2022-03-26T13:49:50Z
```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,163 @@
+/*
+Copyright 2022 The Kubernetes Authors.
+
+Licensed under the Apache License, Version 2.0 (the "License");
+you may not use this file except in compliance with the License.
+You may obtain a copy of the License at
+
+    http://www.apache.org/licenses/LICENSE-2.0
+
+Unless required by applicable law or agreed to in writing, software
+distributed under the License is distributed on an "AS IS" BASIS,
+WITHOUT WARRANTIES OR CONDITIONS OF ANY KIND, either express or implied.
+See the License for the specific language governing permissions and
+limitations under the License.
+*/
+
+package queue
+
+import (
+	"container/heap"
+	"fmt"
+
+	kueue "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/api/v1alpha1"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/workload"
+)
+
+// ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO is the implementation for the ClusterQueue for
+// BestEffortFIFO.
+type ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO struct {
+	*ClusterQueueImpl
+
+	// inadmissibleWorkloads are workloads that have been tried at least once and couldn't be admitted.
+	inadmissibleWorkloads *InadmissibleWorkloads
+}
+
+var _ ClusterQueue = &ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO{}
+
+const BestEffortFIFO = kueue.BestEffortFIFO
+
+func newClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO(cq *kueue.ClusterQueue) (ClusterQueue, error) {
+	cqImpl := ClusterQueueImpl{
+		heap: heapImpl{
+			less:  strictFIFO,
+			items: make(map[string]*heapItem),
+		},
+	}
+
+	cqBE := &ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO{
+		ClusterQueueImpl:      &cqImpl,
+		inadmissibleWorkloads: newInadmissibleWorkloads(),
+	}
+
+	cqBE.Update(cq)
+	return cqBE, nil
+}
+
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) PushOrUpdate(w *kueue.QueuedWorkload) {
+	if oldInfo := cq.inadmissibleWorkloads.get(w); oldInfo != nil {
+		cq.inadmissibleWorkloads.delete(w)
+	}
+
+	item := cq.heap.items[workload.Key(w)]
+	info := *workload.NewInfo(w)
+	if item == nil {
+		heap.Push(&cq.heap, info)
+		return
+	}
+	item.obj = info
+	heap.Fix(&cq.heap, item.index)
+}
+
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) Delete(w *kueue.QueuedWorkload) {
+	item := cq.heap.items[workload.Key(w)]
+	if item != nil {
+		heap.Remove(&cq.heap, item.index)
+	}
+
+	cq.inadmissibleWorkloads.delete(w)
+}
+
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) RequeueWorkload(wInfo *workload.Info) (bool, error) {
+	if err := cq.AddInadmissibleIfNotPresent(wInfo); err != nil {
+		return false, err
+	}
+	return true, nil
+}
+
+// AddInadmissibleIfNotPresent inserts a workload that cannot be admitted into
+// the inadmissibleWorkloads in ClusterQueue, unless it is already in the queue.
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) AddInadmissibleIfNotPresent(wInfo *workload.Info) error {
+	w := wInfo.Obj
+	if cq.inadmissibleWorkloads.get(w) != nil {
+		return fmt.Errorf("workload %v is already present in inadmissibleWorkloads", workload.Key(w))
+	}
+
+	if _, exist := cq.heap.Get(wInfo); exist {
+		return fmt.Errorf("workload %v is already present in the clusterqueue heap", workload.Key(w))
+	}
+
+	cq.inadmissibleWorkloads.addOrUpdate(wInfo)
+	return nil
+}
+
+// QueueAllInadmissibleWorkloads moves all workloads from inadmissibleWorkloads to heap.
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) QueueAllInadmissibleWorkloads() bool {
+	inadmissibleWorkloads := make([]*workload.Info, 0, len(cq.inadmissibleWorkloads.workloads))
+	for _, pInfo := range cq.inadmissibleWorkloads.workloads {
+		inadmissibleWorkloads = append(inadmissibleWorkloads, pInfo)
+	}
+	queued := false
+	for _, wInfo := range inadmissibleWorkloads {
+		w := wInfo.Obj
+		heap.Push(&cq.heap, *wInfo)
+		cq.inadmissibleWorkloads.delete(w)
+		queued = true
+	}
+	return queued
+}
+
+// InadmissibleWorkloads implementation inspired by
+// https://github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes/blob/master/pkg/scheduler/internal/queue/queue.go
+
+// InadmissibleWorkloads holds workloads that cannot be scheduled.
+// This data structure is used to implement inadmissibleWorkloads.
+type InadmissibleWorkloads struct {
```

  this type is just a regular map and its member functions are regular map operations, it is not worth wrapping it as a type, especially that it is an one.

```diff
+See the License for the specific language governing permissions and
+limitations under the License.
+*/
+
+package queue
+
+import (
+	"container/heap"
+	"fmt"
+
+	kueue "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/api/v1alpha1"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/workload"
+)
+
+// ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO is the implementation for the ClusterQueue for
+// BestEffortFIFO.
+type ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO struct {
+	*ClusterQueueImpl
+
+	// inadmissibleWorkloads are workloads that have been tried at least once and couldn't be admitted.
+	inadmissibleWorkloads *InadmissibleWorkloads
+}
+
+var _ ClusterQueue = &ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO{}
+
+const BestEffortFIFO = kueue.BestEffortFIFO
+
+func newClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO(cq *kueue.ClusterQueue) (ClusterQueue, error) {
+	cqImpl := ClusterQueueImpl{
+		heap: heapImpl{
+			less:  strictFIFO,
+			items: make(map[string]*heapItem),
+		},
+	}
+
+	cqBE := &ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO{
+		ClusterQueueImpl:      &cqImpl,
+		inadmissibleWorkloads: newInadmissibleWorkloads(),
+	}
+
+	cqBE.Update(cq)
+	return cqBE, nil
+}
+
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) PushOrUpdate(w *kueue.QueuedWorkload) {
+	if oldInfo := cq.inadmissibleWorkloads.get(w); oldInfo != nil {
+		cq.inadmissibleWorkloads.delete(w)
+	}
+
+	item := cq.heap.items[workload.Key(w)]
+	info := *workload.NewInfo(w)
+	if item == nil {
+		heap.Push(&cq.heap, info)
+		return
+	}
+	item.obj = info
+	heap.Fix(&cq.heap, item.index)
+}
+
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) Delete(w *kueue.QueuedWorkload) {
+	item := cq.heap.items[workload.Key(w)]
+	if item != nil {
+		heap.Remove(&cq.heap, item.index)
+	}
+
+	cq.inadmissibleWorkloads.delete(w)
+}
+
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) RequeueWorkload(wInfo *workload.Info) (bool, error) {
```

  Sorry the reply should be here. 
  I considered this in the first version. But it's hard to determine if the workload is new or re-queued.
  One idea is to add a flag in workload info to be updated if the scheduling fails.

- **pkg/queue/cluster_queue_interface.go:59** by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) — 2022-03-28T16:00:45Z
```diff
@@ -50,6 +52,15 @@ type ClusterQueue interface {
 	// queue is empty.
 	Pop() *workload.Info
 
+	// RequeueWorkload pushes the workload back to ClusterQueue after scheduling failure.
+	RequeueWorkload(*workload.Info) (bool, error)
+	// AddInadmissibleIfNotPresent inserts a workload that cannot be admitted into
+	// the inadmissibleWorkloads in ClusterQueue, unless it is already in the queue.
+	AddInadmissibleIfNotPresent(*workload.Info) error
```

  We should only have the methods that the scheduler needs in the interface.
  
  `AddInadmissibleIfNotPresent` and `RequeIfNotPresent` (previously named `PushIfNotPresent`).
  
  The implementation of StrictFIFO should be that `AddInadmissibleIfNotPresent` just calls `RequeIfNotPresent`.
  
  `PushOrUpdate` is what you would use to receive objects from the controllers, and that will create a `workload.Info` internally. The scheduler needs to push `workload.Info` objects as we might want to carry information for the next scheduling attempts.

```diff
+// ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO is the implementation for the ClusterQueue for
```

```diff
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) PushOrUpdate(w *kueue.QueuedWorkload) {
```

### Review by [@denkensk](https://github.com/denkensk) (commented) — 2022-03-30T07:10:04Z

- **pkg/queue/clsuter_queue_best_effort_fifo.go:125** by [@denkensk](https://github.com/denkensk) — 2022-03-30T07:10:04Z
```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,163 @@
+/*
+Copyright 2022 The Kubernetes Authors.
+
+Licensed under the Apache License, Version 2.0 (the "License");
+you may not use this file except in compliance with the License.
+You may obtain a copy of the License at
+
+    http://www.apache.org/licenses/LICENSE-2.0
+
+Unless required by applicable law or agreed to in writing, software
+distributed under the License is distributed on an "AS IS" BASIS,
+WITHOUT WARRANTIES OR CONDITIONS OF ANY KIND, either express or implied.
+See the License for the specific language governing permissions and
+limitations under the License.
+*/
+
+package queue
+
+import (
+	"container/heap"
+	"fmt"
+
+	kueue "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/api/v1alpha1"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/workload"
+)
+
+// ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO is the implementation for the ClusterQueue for
+// BestEffortFIFO.
+type ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO struct {
+	*ClusterQueueImpl
+
+	// inadmissibleWorkloads are workloads that have been tried at least once and couldn't be admitted.
+	inadmissibleWorkloads *InadmissibleWorkloads
+}
+
+var _ ClusterQueue = &ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO{}
+
+const BestEffortFIFO = kueue.BestEffortFIFO
+
+func newClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO(cq *kueue.ClusterQueue) (ClusterQueue, error) {
+	cqImpl := ClusterQueueImpl{
+		heap: heapImpl{
+			less:  strictFIFO,
+			items: make(map[string]*heapItem),
+		},
+	}
+
+	cqBE := &ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO{
+		ClusterQueueImpl:      &cqImpl,
+		inadmissibleWorkloads: newInadmissibleWorkloads(),
+	}
+
+	cqBE.Update(cq)
+	return cqBE, nil
+}
+
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) PushOrUpdate(w *kueue.QueuedWorkload) {
+	if oldInfo := cq.inadmissibleWorkloads.get(w); oldInfo != nil {
+		cq.inadmissibleWorkloads.delete(w)
+	}
+
+	item := cq.heap.items[workload.Key(w)]
+	info := *workload.NewInfo(w)
+	if item == nil {
+		heap.Push(&cq.heap, info)
+		return
+	}
+	item.obj = info
+	heap.Fix(&cq.heap, item.index)
+}
+
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) Delete(w *kueue.QueuedWorkload) {
+	item := cq.heap.items[workload.Key(w)]
+	if item != nil {
+		heap.Remove(&cq.heap, item.index)
+	}
+
+	cq.inadmissibleWorkloads.delete(w)
+}
+
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) RequeueWorkload(wInfo *workload.Info) (bool, error) {
+	if err := cq.AddInadmissibleIfNotPresent(wInfo); err != nil {
+		return false, err
+	}
+	return true, nil
+}
+
+// AddInadmissibleIfNotPresent inserts a workload that cannot be admitted into
+// the inadmissibleWorkloads in ClusterQueue, unless it is already in the queue.
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) AddInadmissibleIfNotPresent(wInfo *workload.Info) error {
+	w := wInfo.Obj
+	if cq.inadmissibleWorkloads.get(w) != nil {
+		return fmt.Errorf("workload %v is already present in inadmissibleWorkloads", workload.Key(w))
+	}
+
+	if _, exist := cq.heap.Get(wInfo); exist {
+		return fmt.Errorf("workload %v is already present in the clusterqueue heap", workload.Key(w))
+	}
+
+	cq.inadmissibleWorkloads.addOrUpdate(wInfo)
+	return nil
+}
+
+// QueueAllInadmissibleWorkloads moves all workloads from inadmissibleWorkloads to heap.
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) QueueAllInadmissibleWorkloads() bool {
+	inadmissibleWorkloads := make([]*workload.Info, 0, len(cq.inadmissibleWorkloads.workloads))
+	for _, pInfo := range cq.inadmissibleWorkloads.workloads {
+		inadmissibleWorkloads = append(inadmissibleWorkloads, pInfo)
+	}
+	queued := false
+	for _, wInfo := range inadmissibleWorkloads {
+		w := wInfo.Obj
+		heap.Push(&cq.heap, *wInfo)
+		cq.inadmissibleWorkloads.delete(w)
+		queued = true
+	}
+	return queued
+}
+
+// InadmissibleWorkloads implementation inspired by
+// https://github.com/kubernetes/kubernetes/blob/master/pkg/scheduler/internal/queue/queue.go
+
+// InadmissibleWorkloads holds workloads that cannot be scheduled.
+// This data structure is used to implement inadmissibleWorkloads.
+type InadmissibleWorkloads struct {
```

  remove the InadmissibleWorkloads object. Just make inadmissibleWorkloads as a regular map.

```diff
+package queue
+
+import (
+	"container/heap"
+	"fmt"
+
+	kueue "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/api/v1alpha1"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/workload"
+)
+
+// ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO is the implementation for the ClusterQueue for
+// BestEffortFIFO.
+type ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO struct {
+	*ClusterQueueImpl
+
+	// inadmissibleWorkloads are workloads that have been tried at least once and couldn't be admitted.
+	inadmissibleWorkloads *InadmissibleWorkloads
+}
+
+var _ ClusterQueue = &ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO{}
+
+const BestEffortFIFO = kueue.BestEffortFIFO
+
+func newClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO(cq *kueue.ClusterQueue) (ClusterQueue, error) {
+	cqImpl := ClusterQueueImpl{
+		heap: heapImpl{
+			less:  strictFIFO,
+			items: make(map[string]*heapItem),
+		},
+	}
+
+	cqBE := &ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO{
+		ClusterQueueImpl:      &cqImpl,
+		inadmissibleWorkloads: newInadmissibleWorkloads(),
+	}
+
+	cqBE.Update(cq)
+	return cqBE, nil
+}
+
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) PushOrUpdate(w *kueue.QueuedWorkload) {
+	if oldInfo := cq.inadmissibleWorkloads.get(w); oldInfo != nil {
+		cq.inadmissibleWorkloads.delete(w)
+	}
+
+	item := cq.heap.items[workload.Key(w)]
+	info := *workload.NewInfo(w)
+	if item == nil {
+		heap.Push(&cq.heap, info)
+		return
+	}
+	item.obj = info
+	heap.Fix(&cq.heap, item.index)
+}
+
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) Delete(w *kueue.QueuedWorkload) {
+	item := cq.heap.items[workload.Key(w)]
+	if item != nil {
+		heap.Remove(&cq.heap, item.index)
+	}
+
+	cq.inadmissibleWorkloads.delete(w)
+}
+
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) RequeueWorkload(wInfo *workload.Info) (bool, error) {
```

  I leave the function AddInadmissibleIfNotPresent and QueueInadmissibleWorkloads only.

```diff
+
+// ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO is the implementation for the ClusterQueue for
+// BestEffortFIFO.
+type ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO struct {
+	*ClusterQueueImpl
+
+	// inadmissibleWorkloads are workloads that have been tried at least once and couldn't be admitted.
+	inadmissibleWorkloads *InadmissibleWorkloads
+}
+
+var _ ClusterQueue = &ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO{}

+const BestEffortFIFO = kueue.BestEffortFIFO

+func newClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO(cq *kueue.ClusterQueue) (ClusterQueue, error) {
+	cqImpl := ClusterQueueImpl{
+		heap: heapImpl{
+			less:  strictFIFO,
+			items: make(map[string]*heapItem),
+		},
+	}
+
+	cqBE := &ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO{
+		ClusterQueueImpl:      &cqImpl,
+		inadmissibleWorkloads: newInadmissibleWorkloads(),
+	}
+
+	cqBE.Update(cq)
+	return cqBE, nil
+}
+
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) PushOrUpdate(w *kueue.QueuedWorkload) {
+	if oldInfo := cq.inadmissibleWorkloads.get(w); oldInfo != nil {
+		cq.inadmissibleWorkloads.delete(w)
+	}
+
+	item := cq.heap.items[workload.Key(w)]
+	info := *workload.NewInfo(w)
+	if item == nil {
+		heap.Push(&cq.heap, info)
+		return
+	}
+	item.obj = info
+	heap.Fix(&cq.heap, item.index)
+}
+
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) Delete(w *kueue.QueuedWorkload) {
+	item := cq.heap.items[workload.Key(w)]
+	if item != nil {
+		heap.Remove(&cq.heap, item.index)
+	}
+
+	cq.inadmissibleWorkloads.delete(w)
+}
+
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) RequeueWorkload(wInfo *workload.Info) (bool, error) {
+	if err := cq.AddInadmissibleIfNotPresent(wInfo); err != nil {
+		return false, err
+	}
+	return true, nil
+}
+
+// AddInadmissibleIfNotPresent inserts a workload that cannot be admitted into
+// the inadmissibleWorkloads in ClusterQueue, unless it is already in the queue.
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) AddInadmissibleIfNotPresent(wInfo *workload.Info) error {
```

  I roll `RequeueWorkload` into  `AddInadmissibleIfNotPresent` as a single function.

```diff
+
+// ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO is the implementation for the ClusterQueue for
+// BestEffortFIFO.
+type ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO struct {
+	*ClusterQueueImpl
+
+	// inadmissibleWorkloads are workloads that have been tried at least once and couldn't be admitted.
+	inadmissibleWorkloads map[string]*workload.Info
+}
+
+var _ ClusterQueue = &ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO{}
+
+const BestEffortFIFO = kueue.BestEffortFIFO
+
+func newClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO(cq *kueue.ClusterQueue) (ClusterQueue, error) {
+	cqImpl := ClusterQueueImpl{
+		heap: heapImpl{
+			less:  byCreationTime,
+			items: make(map[string]*heapItem),
+		},
+	}
+
+	cqBE := &ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO{
+		ClusterQueueImpl:      &cqImpl,
+		inadmissibleWorkloads: make(map[string]*workload.Info),
+	}
+
+	cqBE.Update(cq)
+	return cqBE, nil
+}
+
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) PushOrUpdate(w *kueue.QueuedWorkload) {
+	key := workload.Key(w)
+	oldInfo := cq.inadmissibleWorkloads[key]
+	if oldInfo != nil {
+		if isWorkloadUpdated(oldInfo.Obj, w) {
+			delete(cq.inadmissibleWorkloads, key)
+		} else {
+			cq.inadmissibleWorkloads[key] = workload.NewInfo(w)
+			return
+		}
+	}
+
+	(*ClusterQueueImpl).PushOrUpdate(cq.ClusterQueueImpl, w)
+}
+
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) Delete(w *kueue.QueuedWorkload) {
+	delete(cq.inadmissibleWorkloads, workload.Key(w))
+
```

- **pkg/queue/cluster_queue_best_effort_fifo_test.go:121** by [@ahg-g](https://github.com/ahg-g) — 2022-03-30T16:59:37Z
```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,127 @@
+/*
+Copyright 2022 The Kubernetes Authors.
+
+Licensed under the Apache License, Version 2.0 (the "License");
+you may not use this file except in compliance with the License.
+You may obtain a copy of the License at
+
+    http://www.apache.org/licenses/LICENSE-2.0
+
+Unless required by applicable law or agreed to in writing, software
+distributed under the License is distributed on an "AS IS" BASIS,
+WITHOUT WARRANTIES OR CONDITIONS OF ANY KIND, either express or implied.
+See the License for the specific language governing permissions and
+limitations under the License.
+*/
+
+package queue
+
+import (
+	"testing"
+
+	"github.com/google/go-cmp/cmp"
+	"k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/util/sets"
+
+	kueue "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/api/v1alpha1"
+	utiltesting "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/util/testing"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/workload"
+)
+
+func TestClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO(t *testing.T) {
+	clusterQueue := utiltesting.MakeClusterQueue("cq").QueueingStrategy(
+		kueue.BestEffortFIFO).Obj()
+	var workloads = []*kueue.QueuedWorkload{
+		utiltesting.MakeQueuedWorkload("w1", "ns1").Queue("q1").Obj(),
+		utiltesting.MakeQueuedWorkload("w2", "ns2").Queue("q2").Obj(),
+	}
+	var updatedWorkloads = make([]*kueue.QueuedWorkload, len(workloads))
+
+	updatedWorkloads[0] = workloads[0].DeepCopy()
+	updatedWorkloads[0].Spec.QueueName = "q2"
+	updatedWorkloads[1] = workloads[1].DeepCopy()
+	updatedWorkloads[1].Spec.QueueName = "q1"
+
+	tests := []struct {
+		name                       string
+		workloadsToAdd             []*kueue.QueuedWorkload
+		inadmissibleWorkloadsToAdd []*workload.Info
+		workloadToUpdate           []*kueue.QueuedWorkload
+		workloadsToDelete          []*kueue.QueuedWorkload
+		QueueInadmissibleWorkloads bool
+		expectWorkloads            sets.String
+	}{
+		{
+			name:                       "add, update, delete workload",
+			workloadsToAdd:             []*kueue.QueuedWorkload{workloads[0], workloads[1]},
+			inadmissibleWorkloadsToAdd: []*workload.Info{},
+			workloadToUpdate:           []*kueue.QueuedWorkload{updatedWorkloads[0]},
+			workloadsToDelete:          []*kueue.QueuedWorkload{workloads[0]},
+			QueueInadmissibleWorkloads: false,
+			expectWorkloads:            sets.NewString(workloads[1].Name),
+		},
+		{
+			name:                       "add inadmissible workload and update",
+			workloadsToAdd:             []*kueue.QueuedWorkload{workloads[0]},
+			inadmissibleWorkloadsToAdd: []*workload.Info{workload.NewInfo(workloads[1])},
+			workloadToUpdate:           []*kueue.QueuedWorkload{updatedWorkloads[1]},
+			workloadsToDelete:          []*kueue.QueuedWorkload{},
+			QueueInadmissibleWorkloads: false,
+			expectWorkloads:            sets.NewString(workloads[0].Name, workloads[1].Name),
+		},
+		{
+			name:                       "add inadmissible workload and move inadmissible workload back to heap",
+			workloadsToAdd:             []*kueue.QueuedWorkload{workloads[0]},
+			inadmissibleWorkloadsToAdd: []*workload.Info{workload.NewInfo(workloads[1])},
+			workloadToUpdate:           []*kueue.QueuedWorkload{},
+			workloadsToDelete:          []*kueue.QueuedWorkload{},
+			QueueInadmissibleWorkloads: true,
+			expectWorkloads:            sets.NewString(workloads[0].Name, workloads[1].Name),
+		},
+		{
+			name:                       "add, delete inadmissible workload and move inadmissible workload back to heap",
+			workloadsToAdd:             []*kueue.QueuedWorkload{workloads[0]},
+			inadmissibleWorkloadsToAdd: []*workload.Info{workload.NewInfo(workloads[1])},
+			workloadToUpdate:           []*kueue.QueuedWorkload{},
+			workloadsToDelete:          []*kueue.QueuedWorkload{workloads[1]},
+			QueueInadmissibleWorkloads: true,
+			expectWorkloads:            sets.NewString(workloads[0].Name),
+		},
+	}
+
+	for _, test := range tests {
+		t.Run(test.name, func(t *testing.T) {
+			cq, err := newClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO(clusterQueue)
+			if err != nil {
+				t.Fatalf("Failed creating ClusterQueue %v", err)
+			}
+
+			for _, w := range test.workloadsToAdd {
+				cq.PushOrUpdate(w)
+			}
+
+			for _, w := range test.inadmissibleWorkloadsToAdd {
+				_, err := cq.AddInadmissibleIfNotPresent(w)
+				if err != nil {
+					t.Fatalf("Failed adding inadmissible workloads %v", err)
+				}
+			}
+
+			for _, w := range test.workloadToUpdate {
+				cq.PushOrUpdate(w)
+			}
+
+			for _, w := range test.workloadsToDelete {
+				cq.Delete(w)
+			}
+
+			if test.QueueInadmissibleWorkloads {
+				cq.QueueInadmissibleWorkloads()
+			}
+
+			result, _ := cq.Dump()
```

  ```suggestion
  			gotWorkloads, _ := cq.Dump()
  ```


  While removing the check at line 140 above is ok, invoking this here is unexpected; I think we should have a function in queue manager that given an "event", it moves indadmissible workloads; we invoke this function explicitly here and in the Delete callback above. We can start with a simple API for this function, just explicitly pass in a `kueue.QueuedWorkload` type.

- **pkg/queue/cluster_queue_best_effort_fifo.go:75** by [@denkensk](https://github.com/denkensk) — 2022-03-31T07:18:27Z
```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,123 @@
+/*
+Copyright 2022 The Kubernetes Authors.
+
+Licensed under the Apache License, Version 2.0 (the "License");
+you may not use this file except in compliance with the License.
+You may obtain a copy of the License at
+
+    http://www.apache.org/licenses/LICENSE-2.0
+
+Unless required by applicable law or agreed to in writing, software
+distributed under the License is distributed on an "AS IS" BASIS,
+WITHOUT WARRANTIES OR CONDITIONS OF ANY KIND, either express or implied.
+See the License for the specific language governing permissions and
+limitations under the License.
+*/
+
+package queue
+
+import (
+	"container/heap"
+	"fmt"
+	"reflect"
+
+	kueue "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/api/v1alpha1"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/workload"
+)
+
+// ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO is the implementation for the ClusterQueue for
+// BestEffortFIFO.
+type ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO struct {
+	*ClusterQueueImpl
+
+	// inadmissibleWorkloads are workloads that have been tried at least once and couldn't be admitted.
+	inadmissibleWorkloads map[string]*workload.Info
+}
+
+var _ ClusterQueue = &ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO{}
+
+const BestEffortFIFO = kueue.BestEffortFIFO
+
+func newClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO(cq *kueue.ClusterQueue) (ClusterQueue, error) {
+	cqImpl := ClusterQueueImpl{
+		heap: heapImpl{
+			less:  byCreationTime,
+			items: make(map[string]*heapItem),
+		},
+	}
+
+	cqBE := &ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO{
+		ClusterQueueImpl:      &cqImpl,
+		inadmissibleWorkloads: make(map[string]*workload.Info),
+	}
+
+	cqBE.Update(cq)
+	return cqBE, nil
+}
+
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) PushOrUpdate(w *kueue.QueuedWorkload) {
+	key := workload.Key(w)
+	oldInfo := cq.inadmissibleWorkloads[key]
+	if oldInfo != nil {
+		if isWorkloadUpdated(oldInfo.Obj, w) {
+			delete(cq.inadmissibleWorkloads, key)
+		} else {
+			cq.inadmissibleWorkloads[key] = workload.NewInfo(w)
+			return
+		}
+	}
+
+	(*ClusterQueueImpl).PushOrUpdate(cq.ClusterQueueImpl, w)
+}
+
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) Delete(w *kueue.QueuedWorkload) {
+	delete(cq.inadmissibleWorkloads, workload.Key(w))
+
```

  Done

```diff
+	updatedWorkloads[0].Spec.QueueName = "q2"
+	updatedWorkloads[1] = workloads[1].DeepCopy()
+	updatedWorkloads[1].Spec.QueueName = "q1"
```

- **pkg/queue/cluster_queue_best_effort_fifo_test.go:121** by [@denkensk](https://github.com/denkensk) — 2022-03-31T07:19:06Z
```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,127 @@
+/*
+Copyright 2022 The Kubernetes Authors.
+

+you may not use this file except in compliance with the License.
+You may obtain a copy of the License at

+

+WITHOUT WARRANTIES OR CONDITIONS OF ANY KIND, either express or implied.
+See the License for the specific language governing permissions and
+limitations under the License.
+*/
+
+package queue
+
+import (
+	"testing"
+
+	"github.com/google/go-cmp/cmp"
+	"k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/util/sets"
+
+	kueue "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/api/v1alpha1"
+	utiltesting "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/util/testing"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/workload"
+)
+
+func TestClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO(t *testing.T) {
+	clusterQueue := utiltesting.MakeClusterQueue("cq").QueueingStrategy(
+		kueue.BestEffortFIFO).Obj()
+	var workloads = []*kueue.QueuedWorkload{
+		utiltesting.MakeQueuedWorkload("w1", "ns1").Queue("q1").Obj(),
+		utiltesting.MakeQueuedWorkload("w2", "ns2").Queue("q2").Obj(),
+	}
+	var updatedWorkloads = make([]*kueue.QueuedWorkload, len(workloads))
+
+	updatedWorkloads[0] = workloads[0].DeepCopy()
+	updatedWorkloads[0].Spec.QueueName = "q2"
+	updatedWorkloads[1] = workloads[1].DeepCopy()
+	updatedWorkloads[1].Spec.QueueName = "q1"
+
+	tests := []struct {
+		name                       string
+		workloadsToAdd             []*kueue.QueuedWorkload
+		inadmissibleWorkloadsToAdd []*workload.Info
+		workloadToUpdate           []*kueue.QueuedWorkload
+		workloadsToDelete          []*kueue.QueuedWorkload
+		QueueInadmissibleWorkloads bool
+		expectWorkloads            sets.String
+	}{
+		{
+			name:                       "add, update, delete workload",
+			workloadsToAdd:             []*kueue.QueuedWorkload{workloads[0], workloads[1]},
+			inadmissibleWorkloadsToAdd: []*workload.Info{},
+			workloadToUpdate:           []*kueue.QueuedWorkload{updatedWorkloads[0]},
+			workloadsToDelete:          []*kueue.QueuedWorkload{workloads[0]},
+			QueueInadmissibleWorkloads: false,
+			expectWorkloads:            sets.NewString(workloads[1].Name),
+		},
+		{
+			name:                       "add inadmissible workload and update",
+			workloadsToAdd:             []*kueue.QueuedWorkload{workloads[0]},
+			inadmissibleWorkloadsToAdd: []*workload.Info{workload.NewInfo(workloads[1])},
+			workloadToUpdate:           []*kueue.QueuedWorkload{updatedWorkloads[1]},
+			workloadsToDelete:          []*kueue.QueuedWorkload{},
+			QueueInadmissibleWorkloads: false,
+			expectWorkloads:            sets.NewString(workloads[0].Name, workloads[1].Name),
+		},
+		{
+			name:                       "add inadmissible workload and move inadmissible workload back to heap",
+			workloadsToAdd:             []*kueue.QueuedWorkload{workloads[0]},
+			inadmissibleWorkloadsToAdd: []*workload.Info{workload.NewInfo(workloads[1])},
+			workloadToUpdate:           []*kueue.QueuedWorkload{},
+			workloadsToDelete:          []*kueue.QueuedWorkload{},
+			QueueInadmissibleWorkloads: true,
+			expectWorkloads:            sets.NewString(workloads[0].Name, workloads[1].Name),
+		},
+		{
+			name:                       "add, delete inadmissible workload and move inadmissible workload back to heap",
+			workloadsToAdd:             []*kueue.QueuedWorkload{workloads[0]},
+			inadmissibleWorkloadsToAdd: []*workload.Info{workload.NewInfo(workloads[1])},
+			workloadToUpdate:           []*kueue.QueuedWorkload{},
+			workloadsToDelete:          []*kueue.QueuedWorkload{workloads[1]},
+			QueueInadmissibleWorkloads: true,
+			expectWorkloads:            sets.NewString(workloads[0].Name),
+		},
+	}
+
+	for _, test := range tests {
+		t.Run(test.name, func(t *testing.T) {
+			cq, err := newClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO(clusterQueue)
+			if err != nil {
+				t.Fatalf("Failed creating ClusterQueue %v", err)
+			}
+
+			for _, w := range test.workloadsToAdd {
+				cq.PushOrUpdate(w)
+			}
+
+			for _, w := range test.inadmissibleWorkloadsToAdd {
+				_, err := cq.AddInadmissibleIfNotPresent(w)
+				if err != nil {
+					t.Fatalf("Failed adding inadmissible workloads %v", err)
+				}
+			}
+
+			for _, w := range test.workloadToUpdate {
+				cq.PushOrUpdate(w)
+			}
+
+			for _, w := range test.workloadsToDelete {
+				cq.Delete(w)
+			}
+
+			if test.QueueInadmissibleWorkloads {
+				cq.QueueInadmissibleWorkloads()
+			}
+
+			result, _ := cq.Dump()
```

### Review by [@denkensk](https://github.com/denkensk) (commented) — 2022-03-31T07:19:31Z

- **pkg/queue/cluster_queue_best_effort_fifo.go:75** by [@denkensk](https://github.com/denkensk) — 2022-03-31T07:19:31Z
```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,123 @@
+/*
+Copyright 2022 The Kubernetes Authors.
+
+Licensed under the Apache License, Version 2.0 (the "License");
+you may not use this file except in compliance with the License.
+You may obtain a copy of the License at
+
+    http://www.apache.org/licenses/LICENSE-2.0
+
+Unless required by applicable law or agreed to in writing, software
+distributed under the License is distributed on an "AS IS" BASIS,
+WITHOUT WARRANTIES OR CONDITIONS OF ANY KIND, either express or implied.
+See the License for the specific language governing permissions and
+limitations under the License.
+*/
+
+package queue
+
+import (
+	"container/heap"
+	"fmt"
+	"reflect"
+
+	kueue "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/api/v1alpha1"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/workload"
+)
+
+// ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO is the implementation for the ClusterQueue for
+// BestEffortFIFO.
+type ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO struct {
+	*ClusterQueueImpl
+
+	// inadmissibleWorkloads are workloads that have been tried at least once and couldn't be admitted.
+	inadmissibleWorkloads map[string]*workload.Info
+}
+
+var _ ClusterQueue = &ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO{}
+
+const BestEffortFIFO = kueue.BestEffortFIFO
+
+func newClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO(cq *kueue.ClusterQueue) (ClusterQueue, error) {
+	cqImpl := ClusterQueueImpl{
+		heap: heapImpl{
+			less:  byCreationTime,
+			items: make(map[string]*heapItem),
+		},
+	}
+
+	cqBE := &ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO{
+		ClusterQueueImpl:      &cqImpl,
+		inadmissibleWorkloads: make(map[string]*workload.Info),
+	}
+
+	cqBE.Update(cq)
+	return cqBE, nil
+}
+
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) PushOrUpdate(w *kueue.QueuedWorkload) {
+	key := workload.Key(w)
+	oldInfo := cq.inadmissibleWorkloads[key]
+	if oldInfo != nil {
+		if isWorkloadUpdated(oldInfo.Obj, w) {
+			delete(cq.inadmissibleWorkloads, key)
+		} else {
+			cq.inadmissibleWorkloads[key] = workload.NewInfo(w)
+			return
+		}
+	}
+
+	(*ClusterQueueImpl).PushOrUpdate(cq.ClusterQueueImpl, w)
+}
+
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) Delete(w *kueue.QueuedWorkload) {
+	delete(cq.inadmissibleWorkloads, workload.Key(w))
+
```

  Done

```diff
 		if err := r.cache.DeleteWorkload(oldWl); err != nil {
 			log.Error(err, "Failed to delete workload from cache")
 		}
+
+		// Clean the workload from the ClusterQueue if it's present and trigger
+		// the relevant inadmissibleWorkloads movement if required.
+		r.queues.DeleteWorkload(oldWl)
```

  I add a new public function in manager. Invoke it in `queuedworkload_controller.go`

```diff
+
+package queue
+
+import (
+	"container/heap"
+	"fmt"
+	"reflect"
+
+	kueue "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/api/v1alpha1"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/workload"
+)
+
+// ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO is the implementation for the ClusterQueue for
+// BestEffortFIFO.
+type ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO struct {
+	*ClusterQueueImpl
+
+	// inadmissibleWorkloads are workloads that have been tried at least once and couldn't be admitted.
+	inadmissibleWorkloads map[string]*workload.Info
+}
+
+var _ ClusterQueue = &ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO{}
+
+const BestEffortFIFO = kueue.BestEffortFIFO
+
+func newClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO(cq *kueue.ClusterQueue) (ClusterQueue, error) {
+	cqImpl := ClusterQueueImpl{
+		heap: heapImpl{
+			less:  byCreationTime,
+			items: make(map[string]*heapItem),
+		},
+	}
+
+	cqBE := &ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO{
+		ClusterQueueImpl:      &cqImpl,
+		inadmissibleWorkloads: make(map[string]*workload.Info),
+	}
+
+	cqBE.Update(cq)
+	return cqBE, nil
+}
+
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) PushOrUpdate(w *kueue.QueuedWorkload) {
+	key := workload.Key(w)
+	oldInfo := cq.inadmissibleWorkloads[key]
+	if oldInfo != nil {
+		if isWorkloadUpdated(oldInfo.Obj, w) {
+			delete(cq.inadmissibleWorkloads, key)
+		} else {
+			cq.inadmissibleWorkloads[key] = workload.NewInfo(w)
+			return
+		}
+	}
+
+	(*ClusterQueueImpl).PushOrUpdate(cq.ClusterQueueImpl, w)
+}
+
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) Delete(w *kueue.QueuedWorkload) {
+	delete(cq.inadmissibleWorkloads, workload.Key(w))
+	(*ClusterQueueImpl).Delete(cq.ClusterQueueImpl, w)
+}
+
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) AddInadmissibleIfNotPresent(wInfo *workload.Info) (bool, error) {
```

  The error and the flag indicate the same thing, just return the flag.

- **pkg/queue/cluster_queue_best_effort_fifo.go:105** by [@ahg-g](https://github.com/ahg-g) — 2022-03-31T18:34:15Z
```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,122 @@
+/*
+Copyright 2022 The Kubernetes Authors.
+
+Licensed under the Apache License, Version 2.0 (the "License");
+you may not use this file except in compliance with the License.
+You may obtain a copy of the License at
+
+    http://www.apache.org/licenses/LICENSE-2.0
+
+Unless required by applicable law or agreed to in writing, software
+distributed under the License is distributed on an "AS IS" BASIS,
+WITHOUT WARRANTIES OR CONDITIONS OF ANY KIND, either express or implied.
+See the License for the specific language governing permissions and
+limitations under the License.
+*/
+
+package queue
+
+import (
+	"container/heap"
+	"fmt"
+	"reflect"
+
+	kueue "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/api/v1alpha1"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/workload"
+)
+
+// ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO is the implementation for the ClusterQueue for
+// BestEffortFIFO.
+type ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO struct {
+	*ClusterQueueImpl
+
+	// inadmissibleWorkloads are workloads that have been tried at least once and couldn't be admitted.
+	inadmissibleWorkloads map[string]*workload.Info
+}
+
+var _ ClusterQueue = &ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO{}
+
+const BestEffortFIFO = kueue.BestEffortFIFO
+
+func newClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO(cq *kueue.ClusterQueue) (ClusterQueue, error) {
+	cqImpl := ClusterQueueImpl{
+		heap: heapImpl{
+			less:  byCreationTime,
+			items: make(map[string]*heapItem),
+		},
+	}
+
+	cqBE := &ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO{
+		ClusterQueueImpl:      &cqImpl,
+		inadmissibleWorkloads: make(map[string]*workload.Info),
+	}
+
+	cqBE.Update(cq)
+	return cqBE, nil
+}
+
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) PushOrUpdate(w *kueue.QueuedWorkload) {
+	key := workload.Key(w)
+	oldInfo := cq.inadmissibleWorkloads[key]
+	if oldInfo != nil {
+		if isWorkloadUpdated(oldInfo.Obj, w) {
+			delete(cq.inadmissibleWorkloads, key)
+		} else {
+			cq.inadmissibleWorkloads[key] = workload.NewInfo(w)
+			return
+		}
+	}
+
+	(*ClusterQueueImpl).PushOrUpdate(cq.ClusterQueueImpl, w)
+}
+
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) Delete(w *kueue.QueuedWorkload) {
+	delete(cq.inadmissibleWorkloads, workload.Key(w))
+	(*ClusterQueueImpl).Delete(cq.ClusterQueueImpl, w)
+}
+
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) AddInadmissibleIfNotPresent(wInfo *workload.Info) (bool, error) {
+	key := workload.Key(wInfo.Obj)
+	if cq.inadmissibleWorkloads[key] != nil {
+		return false, fmt.Errorf("workload %v is already present in inadmissibleWorkloads", key)
+	}
+
+	if _, exist := cq.heap.Get(wInfo); exist {
+		return false, fmt.Errorf("workload %v is already present in the clusterqueue heap", key)
+	}
+
+	cq.inadmissibleWorkloads[key] = wInfo
+
+	return true, nil
+}
+
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) QueueInadmissibleWorkloads() bool {
+	inadmissibleWorkloads := make([]*workload.Info, 0, len(cq.inadmissibleWorkloads))
+	for _, pInfo := range cq.inadmissibleWorkloads {
+		inadmissibleWorkloads = append(inadmissibleWorkloads, pInfo)
+	}
+
+	queued := false
+	for _, wInfo := range inadmissibleWorkloads {
+		heap.Push(&cq.heap, *wInfo)
+		delete(cq.inadmissibleWorkloads, workload.Key(wInfo.Obj))
+		queued = true
+	}
+	return queued
```

  ```suggestion
  	return len(inadmissibleWorkloads) != 0
  ```
  
  and remove the flag

```diff
+		createdJob3 := &batchv1.Job{}
+		gomega.Eventually(func() bool {
+			lookupKey := types.NamespacedName{Name: job3.Name, Namespace: job3.Namespace}
+			return k8sClient.Get(ctx, lookupKey, createdJob3) == nil && !*createdJob3.Spec.Suspend
+		}, framework.Timeout, framework.Interval).Should(gomega.BeTrue())
+		gomega.Expect(createdJob3.Spec.Template.Spec.NodeSelector[instanceKey]).Should(gomega.Equal(onDemandFlavor.Name))
+
+		ginkgo.By("delete job1")
+		gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Delete(ctx, job1)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+		// Simulated deletion of workload by ownerReference of job1.
+		gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Delete(ctx, workload1)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+		gomega.Eventually(func() bool {
+			wl := &kueue.QueuedWorkload{}
+			lookupKey := types.NamespacedName{Name: job1.Name, Namespace: job1.Namespace}
+			if err := k8sClient.Get(ctx, lookupKey, wl); err != nil && apierrors.IsNotFound(err) {
+				return true
+			}
+			return false
+		}, framework.Timeout, framework.Interval).Should(gomega.BeTrue())
```

  You don't need this `Eventually` block.

  ```suggestion
  		gomega.Eventually(func() *bool {
  			lookupKey := types.NamespacedName{Name: job1.Name, Namespace: job1.Namespace}
  			gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, lookupKey, createdJob1)).Should(gomega.Succeed()) 
                           return createdJob1.Spec.Suspend
  		}, framework.Timeout, framework.Interval).Should(gomega.Equal(pointer.Bool(false))
  ```

- **pkg/queue/cluster_queue_best_effort_fifo.go:78** by [@denkensk](https://github.com/denkensk) — 2022-04-01T14:45:28Z
```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,122 @@
+/*
+Copyright 2022 The Kubernetes Authors.
+
+Licensed under the Apache License, Version 2.0 (the "License");
+you may not use this file except in compliance with the License.
+You may obtain a copy of the License at
+

+
+Unless required by applicable law or agreed to in writing, software
+distributed under the License is distributed on an "AS IS" BASIS,
+WITHOUT WARRANTIES OR CONDITIONS OF ANY KIND, either express or implied.
+See the License for the specific language governing permissions and
+limitations under the License.
+*/
+
+package queue
+
+import (
+	"container/heap"
+	"fmt"
+	"reflect"
+
+	kueue "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/api/v1alpha1"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/workload"
+)
+
+// ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO is the implementation for the ClusterQueue for
+// BestEffortFIFO.
+type ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO struct {
+	*ClusterQueueImpl
+
+	// inadmissibleWorkloads are workloads that have been tried at least once and couldn't be admitted.
+	inadmissibleWorkloads map[string]*workload.Info
+}
+
+var _ ClusterQueue = &ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO{}
+
+const BestEffortFIFO = kueue.BestEffortFIFO
+
+func newClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO(cq *kueue.ClusterQueue) (ClusterQueue, error) {
+	cqImpl := ClusterQueueImpl{
+		heap: heapImpl{
+			less:  byCreationTime,
+			items: make(map[string]*heapItem),
+		},
+	}
+
+	cqBE := &ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO{
+		ClusterQueueImpl:      &cqImpl,
+		inadmissibleWorkloads: make(map[string]*workload.Info),
+	}
+
+	cqBE.Update(cq)
+	return cqBE, nil
+}
+
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) PushOrUpdate(w *kueue.QueuedWorkload) {
+	key := workload.Key(w)
+	oldInfo := cq.inadmissibleWorkloads[key]
+	if oldInfo != nil {
+		if isWorkloadUpdated(oldInfo.Obj, w) {
+			delete(cq.inadmissibleWorkloads, key)
+		} else {
+			cq.inadmissibleWorkloads[key] = workload.NewInfo(w)
+			return
+		}
+	}
+
+	(*ClusterQueueImpl).PushOrUpdate(cq.ClusterQueueImpl, w)
+}
+
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) Delete(w *kueue.QueuedWorkload) {
+	delete(cq.inadmissibleWorkloads, workload.Key(w))
+	(*ClusterQueueImpl).Delete(cq.ClusterQueueImpl, w)
+}
+
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) AddInadmissibleIfNotPresent(wInfo *workload.Info) (bool, error) {
```

```diff
+func (m *Manager) RequeueWorkload(ctx context.Context, info *workload.Info) (bool, error) {
```

### Review by [@denkensk](https://github.com/denkensk) (commented) — 2022-04-01T14:45:36Z

- **pkg/queue/cluster_queue_best_effort_fifo.go:105** by [@denkensk](https://github.com/denkensk) — 2022-04-01T14:45:36Z
```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,122 @@
+/*
+Copyright 2022 The Kubernetes Authors.
+
+Licensed under the Apache License, Version 2.0 (the "License");
+you may not use this file except in compliance with the License.
+You may obtain a copy of the License at
+
+    http://www.apache.org/licenses/LICENSE-2.0
+
+Unless required by applicable law or agreed to in writing, software
+distributed under the License is distributed on an "AS IS" BASIS,
+WITHOUT WARRANTIES OR CONDITIONS OF ANY KIND, either express or implied.
+See the License for the specific language governing permissions and
+limitations under the License.
+*/
+
+package queue
+
+import (
+	"container/heap"
+	"fmt"
+	"reflect"
+
+	kueue "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/api/v1alpha1"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/workload"
+)
+
+// ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO is the implementation for the ClusterQueue for
+// BestEffortFIFO.
+type ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO struct {
+	*ClusterQueueImpl
+
+	// inadmissibleWorkloads are workloads that have been tried at least once and couldn't be admitted.
+	inadmissibleWorkloads map[string]*workload.Info
+}
+
+var _ ClusterQueue = &ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO{}
+
+const BestEffortFIFO = kueue.BestEffortFIFO
+
+func newClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO(cq *kueue.ClusterQueue) (ClusterQueue, error) {
+	cqImpl := ClusterQueueImpl{
+		heap: heapImpl{
+			less:  byCreationTime,
+			items: make(map[string]*heapItem),
+		},
+	}
+
+	cqBE := &ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO{
+		ClusterQueueImpl:      &cqImpl,
+		inadmissibleWorkloads: make(map[string]*workload.Info),
+	}
+
+	cqBE.Update(cq)
+	return cqBE, nil
+}
+
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) PushOrUpdate(w *kueue.QueuedWorkload) {
+	key := workload.Key(w)
+	oldInfo := cq.inadmissibleWorkloads[key]
+	if oldInfo != nil {
+		if isWorkloadUpdated(oldInfo.Obj, w) {
+			delete(cq.inadmissibleWorkloads, key)
+		} else {
+			cq.inadmissibleWorkloads[key] = workload.NewInfo(w)
+			return
+		}
+	}
+
+	(*ClusterQueueImpl).PushOrUpdate(cq.ClusterQueueImpl, w)
+}
+
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) Delete(w *kueue.QueuedWorkload) {
+	delete(cq.inadmissibleWorkloads, workload.Key(w))
+	(*ClusterQueueImpl).Delete(cq.ClusterQueueImpl, w)
+}
+
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) AddInadmissibleIfNotPresent(wInfo *workload.Info) (bool, error) {
+	key := workload.Key(wInfo.Obj)
+	if cq.inadmissibleWorkloads[key] != nil {
+		return false, fmt.Errorf("workload %v is already present in inadmissibleWorkloads", key)
+	}
+
+	if _, exist := cq.heap.Get(wInfo); exist {
+		return false, fmt.Errorf("workload %v is already present in the clusterqueue heap", key)
+	}
+
+	cq.inadmissibleWorkloads[key] = wInfo
+
+	return true, nil
+}
+
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) QueueInadmissibleWorkloads() bool {
+	inadmissibleWorkloads := make([]*workload.Info, 0, len(cq.inadmissibleWorkloads))
+	for _, pInfo := range cq.inadmissibleWorkloads {
+		inadmissibleWorkloads = append(inadmissibleWorkloads, pInfo)
+	}
+
+	queued := false
+	for _, wInfo := range inadmissibleWorkloads {
+		heap.Push(&cq.heap, *wInfo)
+		delete(cq.inadmissibleWorkloads, workload.Key(wInfo.Obj))
+		queued = true
+	}
+	return queued
```

  Done

```diff
+		gomega.Eventually(func() bool {
+			lookupKey := types.NamespacedName{Name: job1.Name, Namespace: job1.Namespace}
+			return k8sClient.Get(ctx, lookupKey, createdJob1) == nil && !*createdJob1.Spec.Suspend
+		}, framework.Timeout, framework.Interval).Should(gomega.BeTrue())
+		gomega.Expect(createdJob1.Spec.Template.Spec.NodeSelector[instanceKey]).Should(gomega.Equal(onDemandFlavor.Name))
+
+		job2 := testing.MakeJob("on-demand-job2", ns.Name).Queue(prodBEQueue.Name).Request(corev1.ResourceCPU, "8").Obj()
+		gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, job2)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+		createdJob2 := &batchv1.Job{}
+		gomega.Consistently(func() bool {
+			lookupKey := types.NamespacedName{Name: job2.Name, Namespace: job2.Namespace}
+			return k8sClient.Get(ctx, lookupKey, createdJob2) == nil && *createdJob2.Spec.Suspend
+		}, framework.ConsistentDuration, framework.Interval).Should(gomega.BeTrue())
+
+		job3 := testing.MakeJob("on-demand-job3", ns.Name).Queue(prodBEQueue.Name).Request(corev1.ResourceCPU, "2").Obj()

+		ginkgo.By("delete job1")
```

```diff
+		gomega.Eventually(func() bool {
+			wl := &kueue.QueuedWorkload{}
+			lookupKey := types.NamespacedName{Name: job1.Name, Namespace: job1.Namespace}

+				return true
+			}
+			return false
+		}, framework.Timeout, framework.Interval).Should(gomega.BeTrue())
```

```diff
+		}, framework.Timeout, framework.Interval).Should(gomega.BeTrue())
```

```diff
+				return true
+			}
+			return false
+		}, framework.Timeout, framework.Interval).Should(gomega.BeTrue())

+		createdJob1 := &batchv1.Job{}
+		gomega.Eventually(func() bool {
+			lookupKey := types.NamespacedName{Name: job1.Name, Namespace: job1.Namespace}
+			return k8sClient.Get(ctx, lookupKey, createdJob1) == nil && !*createdJob1.Spec.Suspend
+		}, framework.Timeout, framework.Interval).Should(gomega.BeTrue())
+		gomega.Expect(createdJob1.Spec.Template.Spec.NodeSelector[instanceKey]).Should(gomega.Equal(onDemandFlavor.Name))
+
+		job2 := testing.MakeJob("on-demand-job2", ns.Name).Queue(prodBEQueue.Name).Request(corev1.ResourceCPU, "8").Obj()
+		gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, job2)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+		createdJob2 := &batchv1.Job{}
+		gomega.Consistently(func() bool {
+			lookupKey := types.NamespacedName{Name: job2.Name, Namespace: job2.Namespace}
+			return k8sClient.Get(ctx, lookupKey, createdJob2) == nil && *createdJob2.Spec.Suspend
+		}, framework.ConsistentDuration, framework.Interval).Should(gomega.BeTrue())
+
+		job3 := testing.MakeJob("on-demand-job3", ns.Name).Queue(prodBEQueue.Name).Request(corev1.ResourceCPU, "2").Obj()
+		gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, job3)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+		createdJob3 := &batchv1.Job{}
+		gomega.Eventually(func() bool {
+			lookupKey := types.NamespacedName{Name: job3.Name, Namespace: job3.Namespace}
+			return k8sClient.Get(ctx, lookupKey, createdJob3) == nil && !*createdJob3.Spec.Suspend
+		}, framework.Timeout, framework.Interval).Should(gomega.BeTrue())
+		gomega.Expect(createdJob3.Spec.Template.Spec.NodeSelector[instanceKey]).Should(gomega.Equal(onDemandFlavor.Name))
+
+		ginkgo.By("delete job1")
```
```diff
+		gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Delete(ctx, job1)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+		// Simulated deletion of workload by ownerReference of job1.
+		gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Delete(ctx, workload1)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+		gomega.Eventually(func() bool {
+			wl := &kueue.QueuedWorkload{}
+			lookupKey := types.NamespacedName{Name: job1.Name, Namespace: job1.Namespace}
+			if err := k8sClient.Get(ctx, lookupKey, wl); err != nil && apierrors.IsNotFound(err) {
+				return true
+			}
+			return false
+		}, framework.Timeout, framework.Interval).Should(gomega.BeTrue())
+
+		gomega.Eventually(func() bool {
+			lookupKey := types.NamespacedName{Name: job2.Name,
+				Namespace: job2.Namespace}
+			return k8sClient.Get(ctx, lookupKey,
+				createdJob2) == nil && !*createdJob2.Spec.Suspend
+		}, framework.Timeout, framework.Interval).Should(gomega.BeTrue())
+		gomega.Expect(createdJob2.Spec.Template.Spec.NodeSelector[instanceKey]).Should(gomega.Equal(onDemandFlavor.Name))
+	})
+
+	ginkgo.It("Should re-enqueue by the delete event of workload belonging to the same Cohort", func() {
+		job1 := testing.MakeJob("on-demand-job1", ns.Name).Queue(prodBEQueue.Name).Request(corev1.ResourceCPU, "8").Obj()
+		gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Create(ctx, job1)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+		workload1 := &kueue.QueuedWorkload{}
+		gomega.Eventually(func() bool {
+			lookupKey := types.NamespacedName{Name: job1.Name, Namespace: job1.Namespace}
+			err := k8sClient.Get(ctx, lookupKey, workload1)
+			return err == nil
+		}, framework.Timeout, framework.Interval).Should(gomega.BeTrue())
```

- **pkg/queue/cluster_queue_best_effort_fifo.go:119** by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) — 2022-04-01T15:32:06Z
```diff
@@ -0,0 +1,120 @@
+/*
+Copyright 2022 The Kubernetes Authors.
+
+Licensed under the Apache License, Version 2.0 (the "License");
+you may not use this file except in compliance with the License.
+You may obtain a copy of the License at
+
+    http://www.apache.org/licenses/LICENSE-2.0
+
+Unless required by applicable law or agreed to in writing, software
+distributed under the License is distributed on an "AS IS" BASIS,
+WITHOUT WARRANTIES OR CONDITIONS OF ANY KIND, either express or implied.
+See the License for the specific language governing permissions and
+limitations under the License.
+*/
+
+package queue
+
+import (
+	"reflect"
+
+	kueue "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/api/v1alpha1"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/workload"
+)
+
+// ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO is the implementation for the ClusterQueue for
+// BestEffortFIFO.
+type ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO struct {
+	*ClusterQueueImpl
+
+	// inadmissibleWorkloads are workloads that have been tried at least once and couldn't be admitted.
+	inadmissibleWorkloads map[string]*workload.Info
+}
+
+var _ ClusterQueue = &ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO{}
+
+const BestEffortFIFO = kueue.BestEffortFIFO
+
+func newClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO(cq *kueue.ClusterQueue) (ClusterQueue, error) {
+	cqImpl := ClusterQueueImpl{
+		heap: heapImpl{
+			less:  byCreationTime,
+			items: make(map[string]*heapItem),
+		},
+	}
+
+	cqBE := &ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO{
+		ClusterQueueImpl:      &cqImpl,
+		inadmissibleWorkloads: make(map[string]*workload.Info),
+	}
+
+	cqBE.Update(cq)
+	return cqBE, nil
+}
+
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) PushOrUpdate(w *kueue.QueuedWorkload) {
+	key := workload.Key(w)
+	oldInfo := cq.inadmissibleWorkloads[key]
+	if oldInfo != nil {
+		// update in place if the workload was inadmissible and didn't change
+		// to potentially become admissible.
+		if !isWorkloadUpdated(oldInfo.Obj, w) {
+			cq.inadmissibleWorkloads[key] = workload.NewInfo(w)
+			return
+		}
+		// otherwise move or update in place in the queue.
+		delete(cq.inadmissibleWorkloads, key)
+	}
+
+	(*ClusterQueueImpl).PushOrUpdate(cq.ClusterQueueImpl, w)
+}
+
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) Delete(w *kueue.QueuedWorkload) {
+	delete(cq.inadmissibleWorkloads, workload.Key(w))
+	(*ClusterQueueImpl).Delete(cq.ClusterQueueImpl, w)
+}
+
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) AddInadmissibleIfNotPresent(wInfo *workload.Info) bool {
+	key := workload.Key(wInfo.Obj)
+	if cq.inadmissibleWorkloads[key] != nil {
+		return false
+	}
+
+	if item := cq.heap.items[key]; item != nil {
+		return false
+	}
+
+	cq.inadmissibleWorkloads[key] = wInfo
+
+	return true
+}
+
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) QueueInadmissibleWorkloads() bool {
+	inadmissibleWorkloads := make([]*workload.Info, 0, len(cq.inadmissibleWorkloads))
+	for _, pInfo := range cq.inadmissibleWorkloads {
+		inadmissibleWorkloads = append(inadmissibleWorkloads, pInfo)
+	}
+
+	for _, wInfo := range inadmissibleWorkloads {
+		(*ClusterQueueImpl).pushIfNotPresent(cq.ClusterQueueImpl, wInfo)
+		delete(cq.inadmissibleWorkloads, workload.Key(wInfo.Obj))
+	}
+	return len(inadmissibleWorkloads) != 0
+}
+
+// isWorkloadUpdated checks if the workload is updated in a way that it may have
+// become schedulable. It drops status of the workload and compares it with old
+// version.
+func isWorkloadUpdated(old, new *kueue.QueuedWorkload) bool {
+	strip := func(workload *kueue.QueuedWorkload) *kueue.QueuedWorkload {
+		w := workload.DeepCopy()
+		w.ResourceVersion = ""
+		w.Generation = 0
+		w.Status = kueue.QueuedWorkloadStatus{}
+		w.ManagedFields = nil
+		w.Finalizers = nil
+		return w
+	}
+	return !reflect.DeepEqual(strip(old), strip(new))
```

  Use `equality.Semantic.DeepEqual` from `k8s.io/apimachinery/pkg/api/equality`

- **pkg/queue/cluster_queue_best_effort_fifo.go:29** by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) — 2022-04-01T15:34:47Z

```diff
+type ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO struct {
+	*ClusterQueueImpl
```


```diff
+package queue

+import (
+	"reflect"

+	kueue "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/api/v1alpha1"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/workload"

+// BestEffortFIFO.

+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) PushOrUpdate(w *kueue.QueuedWorkload) {

+		}
+		// otherwise move or update in place in the queue.
+		delete(cq.inadmissibleWorkloads, key)
+	}
+
+	(*ClusterQueueImpl).PushOrUpdate(cq.ClusterQueueImpl, w)
+}
+
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) Delete(w *kueue.QueuedWorkload) {
+	delete(cq.inadmissibleWorkloads, workload.Key(w))
+	(*ClusterQueueImpl).Delete(cq.ClusterQueueImpl, w)
+}
+
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) AddInadmissibleIfNotPresent(wInfo *workload.Info) bool {
+	key := workload.Key(wInfo.Obj)
+	if cq.inadmissibleWorkloads[key] != nil {
+		return false
+	}
+
+	if item := cq.heap.items[key]; item != nil {
+		return false
+	}
+
+	cq.inadmissibleWorkloads[key] = wInfo
+
+	return true
+}
+
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) QueueInadmissibleWorkloads() bool {
+	inadmissibleWorkloads := make([]*workload.Info, 0, len(cq.inadmissibleWorkloads))
+	for _, pInfo := range cq.inadmissibleWorkloads {
+		inadmissibleWorkloads = append(inadmissibleWorkloads, pInfo)
+	}
+
+	for _, wInfo := range inadmissibleWorkloads {
+		(*ClusterQueueImpl).pushIfNotPresent(cq.ClusterQueueImpl, wInfo)
+		delete(cq.inadmissibleWorkloads, workload.Key(wInfo.Obj))
+	}
+	return len(inadmissibleWorkloads) != 0
+}
+
+// isWorkloadUpdated checks if the workload is updated in a way that it may have
+// become schedulable. It drops status of the workload and compares it with old
+// version.
+func isWorkloadUpdated(old, new *kueue.QueuedWorkload) bool {
+	strip := func(workload *kueue.QueuedWorkload) *kueue.QueuedWorkload {
```

  instead of stripping it, why not just compare the spec only?

```diff
+package queue
+
+import (
+	"reflect"
+
+	kueue "sigs.k8s.io/kueue/api/v1alpha1"
+	"sigs.k8s.io/kueue/pkg/workload"
+)
+
+// ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO is the implementation for the ClusterQueue for
+// BestEffortFIFO.
+type ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO struct {
+	*ClusterQueueImpl
+
+	// inadmissibleWorkloads are workloads that have been tried at least once and couldn't be admitted.
+	inadmissibleWorkloads map[string]*workload.Info
+}
+
+var _ ClusterQueue = &ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO{}
+
+const BestEffortFIFO = kueue.BestEffortFIFO
+
+func newClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO(cq *kueue.ClusterQueue) (ClusterQueue, error) {
+	cqImpl := ClusterQueueImpl{
+		heap: heapImpl{
+			less:  byCreationTime,
+			items: make(map[string]*heapItem),
+		},
+	}
+
+	cqBE := &ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO{
+		ClusterQueueImpl:      &cqImpl,
+		inadmissibleWorkloads: make(map[string]*workload.Info),
+	}
+
+	cqBE.Update(cq)
+	return cqBE, nil
+}
+
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) PushOrUpdate(w *kueue.QueuedWorkload) {
+	key := workload.Key(w)
+	oldInfo := cq.inadmissibleWorkloads[key]
+	if oldInfo != nil {
+		// update in place if the workload was inadmissible and didn't change
+		// to potentially become admissible.
+		if !isWorkloadUpdated(oldInfo.Obj, w) {
+			cq.inadmissibleWorkloads[key] = workload.NewInfo(w)
+			return
+		}
+		// otherwise move or update in place in the queue.
+		delete(cq.inadmissibleWorkloads, key)
+	}
+
+	(*ClusterQueueImpl).PushOrUpdate(cq.ClusterQueueImpl, w)
+}
+
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) Delete(w *kueue.QueuedWorkload) {
+	delete(cq.inadmissibleWorkloads, workload.Key(w))
+	(*ClusterQueueImpl).Delete(cq.ClusterQueueImpl, w)
+}
+
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) AddInadmissibleIfNotPresent(wInfo *workload.Info) bool {
+	key := workload.Key(wInfo.Obj)
+	if cq.inadmissibleWorkloads[key] != nil {
+		return false
+	}
+
+	if item := cq.heap.items[key]; item != nil {
+		return false
+	}
+
+	cq.inadmissibleWorkloads[key] = wInfo
+
+	return true
+}
+
+func (cq *ClusterQueueBestEffortFIFO) QueueInadmissibleWorkloads() bool {
+	inadmissibleWorkloads := make([]*workload.Info, 0, len(cq.inadmissibleWorkloads))
```

  what's this slice for?
  
  It looks like you are just removing everything, so I think you could push everything from the original map and then set it to empty at the end of the function.

- **pkg/queue/cluster_queue_interface.go:53** by [@alculquicondor](https://github.com/alculquicondor) — 2022-04-01T15:53:50Z
```diff
@@ -50,6 +49,13 @@ type ClusterQueue interface {
 	// queue is empty.
 	Pop() *workload.Info
 
+	// AddInadmissibleIfNotPresent inserts a workload that cannot be admitted into
+	// the inadmissibleWorkloads in ClusterQueue, unless it is already in the queue.
```

  this is an implementation detail that doesn't apply to a strictFIFO queue.
  
  Maybe you can say:
  
  inserts a workload that could not be admitted back into the ClusterQueue. The implementation might choose to keep it in temporary placeholder stage where it doesn't compete with other workloads, until cluster events free up quota. The workload should not be reinserted if it's already in the ClusterQueue.

  again, implementation detail. You can refer to this as a notification. Maybe the name could be:
  
  `NotifyPotentialAvailability`
